<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>4.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Pension and Retirement Plans </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Employees of the Food Business participate in both defined contribution
pension plans and defined benefit pension plans. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Defined benefit plans </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Eligible employees of the Food Business are members of the Retirement Plan for Union Employees of Reckitt Benckiser, LLC (the &#147;Union Pension Plan&#148;),
which is a defined benefit pension plan. Certain other current and former employees of the Food Business are members of a multi-employer plan operated by RB, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-union</FONT> defined benefit pension
plan.&nbsp;Additionally, certain senior employees are members of the Reckitt Benckiser LLC executive pension plan. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Food Business&#146;s accounts for
pension and retirement plans in accordance with the authoritative guidance for retirement benefit compensation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Food Business applies defined benefit
plan accounting for its participation in the Union Pension Plan. The Food Business measures its plan assets at fair value and the obligations at the present value of the estimated payments to plan participants. Plan assets consist of a mix of
equities, fixed income funds and real estate funds. Participants earn benefits based on their service and pay. Those estimated payment amounts are determined based on assumptions. Actuarial gains and losses are fully recognized in the combined
statement of income. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following represents the components of net periodic (benefit) cost: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Food Business accounts for its participation in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-union</FONT> defined
benefit pension plan, the Reckitt Benckiser LLC executive pension plan and other post-retirement plans as multi-employer plans. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Contributions </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Food Business&#146; policy for funding the Union Pension Plan is to contribute amounts sufficient to meet minimum funding requirements under employee
benefit and tax laws. No contributions were made in the interim period to June&nbsp;30, 2017 and 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Amounts for post-employment benefits excluding the
Union Pension Plan are included in administrative expenses within the combined statement of income and totaled $1.7&nbsp;million and $1.6&nbsp;million for the six month periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2017 and 2016, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>5.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Share-based Compensation </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain of the Food Business&#146; employees participate in RB&#146;s various
incentive plans. Net income for June&nbsp;30, 2017 and 2016 included <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> share-based compensation expense, within administrative expenses, of $0.7&nbsp;million and $0.7&nbsp;million, respectively, which
related to share options and the restricted share scheme. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>6.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Commitments and Contingencies </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&nbsp;15,&nbsp;2017, the Food Business executed a settlement
agreement with the United Food and Commercial Workers and Employers Food Trades and Industrial Health and Welfare Plan and its trustees (the &#147;fund&#148;) regarding the disputed Health&nbsp;&amp; Welfare contributions due under the Collective
Bargaining Agreement. The settlement agreement comprised of $2.8&nbsp;million for the period to June&nbsp;30, 2017 plus an interest charge of $0.3&nbsp;million. Additionally, an amount of $2.7&nbsp;million was also agreed for the years 2018 &#150;
2021.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The combined interim financial statements for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended
June&nbsp;30, 2017 include a charge within administrative expenses of $0.3&nbsp;million. The liability recognized at June&nbsp;30, 2017 was $3.1&nbsp;million and is included within accrued payroll and other employee related costs. The charge for the
year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016 and the liability recognized at December&nbsp;31, 2016 was $2.8&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As of June&nbsp;30, 2017, there were no
other material changes in the Food Business&#146;s legal proceedings, contractual obligations and commercial commitments outside the ordinary course of business, as set out in the audited combined financial statements and notes thereto for the
fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016, 2015 and 2014 respectively. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>7.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Income Taxes </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The effective income tax rate was 26% for the six months to June&nbsp;30, 2017 and 24% for
the six months to June&nbsp;30, 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Food Business operates in an international environment, accordingly, the combined effective tax rate is a
composite rate reflecting the earnings in various locations and the applicable tax rates. Appropriate provisions have been made in respect of any uncertain tax positions that exist in relation to the Food Business. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>8.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Related Party and Parent Company Transactions </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Historically, RB has provided services to the Food
Business. These services and expenses include finance, legal, tax, treasury, information technology, human resources, communications, employee benefits and incentives, insurance and share based compensation. The combined statements of income also
include a portion of RB&#146;s group costs relating to its operations as a public company, including, but not limited to, corporate governance and board oversight, not historically allocated to the Food Business. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These service charges and corporate expense allocations are based on a number of utilization measures including headcount, revenue, and operating profit.
Management believes that the methods used to allocate expenses to the Food Business are reasonable. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">F-10 </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>11.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Subsequent Events </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Food Business did not have any subsequent events through August&nbsp;4, 2017,
which is the date its unaudited combined interim financial statements were available to be issued, that would require recording or disclosure in the combined financial statements for the period ending June&nbsp;30, 2017, except as disclosed below
and as set out in Note 6. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&nbsp;19, 2017, RB announced that it has entered into an agreement to sell its Food business to McCormick&nbsp;&amp;
Company Inc. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">F-13 </P>

<DOCUMENT>
<TYPE>EX-99.3
<SEQUENCE>5
<FILENAME>d439451dex993.htm
<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.3
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.3</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.3 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Unaudited Pro Forma Condensed Combined Financial Information </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&nbsp;18, 2017, McCormick&nbsp;&amp; Company, Incorporated, a Maryland corporation (&#147;McCormick&#148;), entered into a Stock Purchase Agreement
(the &#147;Agreement&#148;) with The R.T. French&#146;s Food Group Limited, a private limited company incorporated in England and Wales (&#147;French&#146;s Seller&#148;), Reckitt Benckiser LLC, a Delaware limited liability company
(&#147;Tiger&#146;s Milk Seller&#148; and, together with French&#146;s Seller, the &#147;Sellers&#148;), and Reckitt Benckiser Group plc (&#147;Sellers&#146; Parent&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the terms and conditions of the Agreement, at the closing, McCormick will acquire 100% of the outstanding equity interests of each of (i)&nbsp;The
French&#146;s Food Company LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (&#147;French&#146;s US&#148;), (ii)&nbsp;The French&#146;s Food Company, Inc., a Canadian corporation (&#147;French&#146;s Canada&#148;), (iii)&nbsp;The R.T. French&#146;s Food
Company Limited, a private limited company incorporated in England and Wales (&#147;French&#146;s UK&#148;), and (iv)&nbsp;Tiger&#146;s Milk LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (&#147;Tiger&#146;s Milk&#148;), and together with French&#146;s
US, French&#146;s Canada and French&#146;s UK, the &#147;Acquired Business&#148;, which is referred to herein as the &#147;Acquisition&#148;. The aggregate purchase price payable by McCormick is $4.2&nbsp;billion in cash, subject to customary
purchase price adjustments related to the amount of the Acquired Business&#146; cash, debt, net working capital, and transaction expenses as described in the Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The closing of the transaction is subject to customary closing conditions, including the expiration or early termination of the waiting period under the
Hart-Scott-Rodino Antitrust Improvements Act of 1976, as amended. The Agreement contains certain termination rights for the Sellers and McCormick, including if the closing does not occur before 5:00 p.m. New York City time on January&nbsp;18, 2018,
subject to certain extension rights. Subject to the satisfaction of these conditions, McCormick expects to complete the Acquisition before the end of the fiscal year ending November&nbsp;30, 2017. McCormick&#146;s obligation to consummate the
transaction is not subject to any condition related to the availability of financing. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with McCormick&#146;s entry into the Agreement,
McCormick has entered into a commitment letter, dated July&nbsp;18, 2017 (the &#147;Commitment Letter&#148;), with Merrill Lynch, Pierce, Fenner&nbsp;&amp; Smith Incorporated, Bank of America, N.A. (&#147;Bank of America&#148;), and Credit Suisse
Securities (USA) LLC and Credit Suisse AG ( &#147;Credit Suisse&#148;), pursuant to which and subject to the terms and conditions set forth therein, Bank of America and Credit Suisse have agreed to provide a senior unsecured <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">364-day</FONT> bridge loan facility (the &#147;Bridge Facility&#148;) of up to $4.2&nbsp;billion in the aggregate for the purpose of providing the financing necessary to fund all or a portion of the consideration to be
paid pursuant to the terms of the Agreement and related fees and expenses (the &#147;Bridge Loan Commitment&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Bridge Loan Commitment will be
reduced in equivalent amounts upon any incurrence by McCormick of term loans and/or the issuance of equity or notes in a public offering or private placement prior to the consummation of the transaction and loans under the Bridge Facility will be
prepaid in equivalent amounts upon the incurrence by McCormick of term loans and/or the issuance of equity or notes in a public offering or private placement and upon other specified events, in each case subject to certain exceptions set forth in
the Commitment Letter. Although we do not currently expect to make any borrowings under the Bridge Facility, there can be no assurance that such borrowings will not be made. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">McCormick expects to permanently finance the transaction with $3.7&nbsp;billion of new debt, which will include <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-payable</FONT> terms loans and senior unsecured notes issued in the capital markets, and the issuance of $500&nbsp;million of McCormick common stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-voting,</FONT> no par value
(&#147;Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting&#148;).</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with the Acquisition, Sellers have prepared historical
financial information for Reckitt Benckiser Group plc&#146;s food business (the &#147;Food Business&#148;). The Food Business was historically managed together with certain other financing legal entities which are not being acquired in the
Acquisition. Amounts included in the historical financial information related to those entities that are not being acquired as part of the Acquired Business are eliminated as a pro forma adjustment in the unaudited pro forma condensed combined
financial information. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information is based on the historical financial information of
McCormick and the Food Business and has been prepared to reflect the pending Acquisition and related financing transactions, as previously described. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information is provided for informational
purposes only. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements are not necessarily indicative of operating results that would have been
achieved had the Acquisition been completed as of December&nbsp;1, 2015 and does not intend to project the future financial results of McCormick after the Acquisition. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet does not purport to
reflect what our financial condition would have been had the Acquisition closed on May&nbsp;31, 2017 or for any future or historical period. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements and balance sheet do not reflect the cost of
any integration activities or benefits from the Acquisition and synergies that may be derived, both of which may have a material effect on our consolidated results in periods following completion of the Acquisition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">McCormick&#146;s fiscal year ends on November&nbsp;30, while the Food Business&#146; fiscal year ends on December 31. Pursuant to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;11-02(c)(3)</FONT> of Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-X,</FONT> the fiscal years are not being conformed for the purpose of presenting unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial statements,
because the two fiscal year ends are not separated by more than 93 days. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed combined interim balance sheet combines the
unaudited condensed consolidated balance sheet of McCormick as of May&nbsp;31, 2017 and the unaudited combined balance sheet of the Food Business as of June&nbsp;30, 2017. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statement for the year
ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 combines the consolidated income statement of McCormick for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 with the combined statement of income of the Food Business for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016. The interim
unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statement for the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017 combines the unaudited condensed income statement of McCormick for the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017 and the unaudited combined statement of
income of the Food Business for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information should be read
in conjunction with the following information: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" COLSPAN="2" ALIGN="center" STYLE="border-bottom:1.00pt solid #000000"><B>Pro Forma</B><br><B>Adjustments</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Unaudited Pro Forma Condensed Combined Financial Information </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>1. Basis of Presentation and Accounting Policies </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Basis of Presentation </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed
combined financial information presented herein is based on the historical audited consolidated and unaudited condensed consolidated financial information of McCormick and the audited and unaudited combined financial information of the Food
Business, or is derived therefrom. McCormick&#146;s fiscal year ends on November&nbsp;30, while the Food Business&#146; fiscal year ends on December 31. Pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">11-02(c)(3)</FONT> of Regulation <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-X,</FONT> the fiscal years are not being conformed for the purpose of presenting unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial statements, because the two fiscal year ends are not separated by more than 93 days. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet combines the unaudited condensed consolidated balance sheet of McCormick as of May&nbsp;31, 2017 and
the unaudited combined balance sheet of the Food Business as of June&nbsp;30, 2017. The unaudited pro&nbsp;forma condensed combined income statement for the year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 combines the consolidated income statement of McCormick
for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 with the combined statement of income of the Food Business for the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016. The interim unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statement for the six months
ended May&nbsp;31, 2017 combines the unaudited condensed consolidated income statement of McCormick for the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017 and the unaudited combined statement of income of the Food Business for the six months ended June&nbsp;30,
2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pro forma adjustments reflected in the unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet are based on items that are directly attributable to
the pending Acquisition and related financings that are factually supportable. Pro forma adjustments reflected in the unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements are based on items directly attributable to the pending Acquisition and
related financings, and that are factually supportable and expected to have a continuing impact on McCormick. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed combined
income statements are not necessarily indicative of operating results that would have been achieved had the Acquisition been completed as of December&nbsp;1, 2015 and does not intend to project the future financial results of McCormick after the
Acquisition. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet does not purport to reflect what our financial condition would have been had the Acquisition closed on May&nbsp;31, 2017 or for any future or historical period. Additionally, the
unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements and balance sheet do not reflect the cost of any integration activities from the Acquisition and synergies that may be derived from any integration activities, both of which may have a
material effect on our consolidated results in periods following completion of the Acquisition. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Accounting Policies </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Acquisition will be accounted for under the acquisition method of accounting in accordance with the Financial Accounting Standards Board (FASB) Accounting
Standards Codification (ASC) Topic 805, <I>Business Combinations</I>. As the acquirer, McCormick has estimated the fair value of the Food Business&#146; assets acquired and liabilities assumed and conformed the accounting policies of the Food
Business to its own accounting policies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The accounting policies used in the preparation of the unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial
information are those set out in McCormick&#146;s consolidated financial statements as of and for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016. With the information currently available, McCormick has determined
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
that, other than those pro forma adjustments identified, and as more fully described in (h)&nbsp;in Note 4, no other significant adjustments are necessary to conform the Food Business&#146;
combined financial statements to the accounting policies used by McCormick in the preparation of the unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information. Certain reclassification adjustments have been made to the Food Business&#146;
historical unaudited combined balance sheet as of June&nbsp;30, 2017 and unaudited combined statement of income for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017 and year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016 to conform to McCormick&#146;s presentation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At this time, McCormick has not completed detailed valuation analyses to determine the fair values of the acquired assets and liabilities of the Food
Business. Accordingly, the unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information includes a preliminary allocation of the purchase price based on assumptions and estimates that, while considered reasonable under the circumstances, are subject
to changes, which may be material. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">McCormick has not yet completed the due diligence necessary to identify all of the adjustments required to conform the
Food Business&#146; accounting policies or classifications to McCormick&#146;s accounting policies or to identify other items that could significantly impact the purchase price allocation or the assumptions and adjustments made in preparation of
this unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information. Upon completion of this due diligence and detailed valuation analyses, there may be additional increases or decreases to the recorded book values of acquired assets and liabilities
of the Acquired Business, including, but not limited to pension liabilities; property, plant and equipment; and brands and other intangible assets, each of which may give rise to future amounts of depreciation and amortization expense that are not
reflected in this unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information. Accordingly, once the necessary due diligence and valuation analyses have been performed, the final purchase price has been determined and the purchase price allocation
has been finalized, actual results may differ materially from the information presented in this unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>2. Financing Transactions and Assumptions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection
with McCormick&#146;s entry into the Agreement, McCormick entered into a commitment letter, dated July&nbsp;18, 2017 (the &#147;Commitment Letter&#148;), with Merrill Lynch, Pierce, Fenner&nbsp;&amp; Smith Incorporated, Bank of America, N.A.
(&#147;Bank of America&#148;), and Credit Suisse Securities (USA) LLC and Credit Suisse AG ( &#147;Credit Suisse&#148;), pursuant to which and subject to the terms and conditions set forth therein, Bank of America and Credit Suisse have agreed to
provide a senior unsecured <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">364-day</FONT> bridge loan facility (the &#147;Bridge Facility&#148;) of up to $4.2&nbsp;billion in the aggregate for the purpose of providing the financing necessary to fund all or a
portion of the consideration to be paid pursuant to the terms of the Agreement and related fees and expenses. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information presented herein does not contemplate the need for drawing under the
Bridge Facility prior to permanent financing being put in place. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">McCormick expects to permanently finance the Acquisition with $3.7&nbsp;billion of new
debt, which will include <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-payable</FONT> terms loans and senior unsecured notes issued in the capital markets, and $500&nbsp;million in Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting.</FONT> The
unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information assumes that the financing will consist of: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

and has been used to prepare pro forma adjustments in the pro forma unaudited condensed combined financial information. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At this time, McCormick has not completed detailed valuation analyses to determine the fair values of the
acquired assets and liabilities of the Food Business. Accordingly, the unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information includes a preliminary allocation of the purchase price based on assumptions and estimates that, while considered
reasonable under the circumstances, are subject to changes, which may be material. The purchase price will be primarily allocated to indefinite-lived intangible assets, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">finite-lived</FONT> intangible assets and
goodwill. The preliminary allocation of the purchase price results in approximately $2,475&nbsp;million and $120&nbsp;million being allocated to indefinite-lived intangible assets and finite-lived intangible assets, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>4. Unaudited Pro Forma Adjustments to Historical Financial Information </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements include adjustments made to historical financial information that were calculated assuming the
Acquisition had been completed as of December&nbsp;1, 2015. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet includes adjustments made to historical financial information that were calculated assuming the Acquisition had been completed as of
May&nbsp;31, 2017. We have based the unaudited pro forma adjustments upon available information and certain assumptions that we believe are reasonable under the circumstances. The adjustments reflect our preliminary estimates of the purchase price
allocation, which may change materially upon finalization of appraisals and other valuation studies that are in process. Additionally, the unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements and balance sheet do not reflect the cost of any
integration activities from the Acquisition and synergies that may be derived from any integration activities, both of which may have a material effect on our consolidated results in periods following the completion of the Acquisition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following adjustments have been reflected in the unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial information: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet reflects the expected purchase price of the Acquisition and a preliminary allocation of the
purchase price, as more fully detailed in Note 3, based on assumptions and estimates that, while considered reasonable under the circumstances, are subject to changes, which may be material. The purchase price will be primarily allocated to
indefinite-lived intangible assets, finite-lived intangible assets and goodwill. Finite-lived intangible assets are expected to be amortized over weighted average lives of approximately 15 years. The purchase accounting adjustment of approximately
$984&nbsp;million in Other long-term liabilities is primarily related to the estimated deferred tax liability associated with indefinite-lived and finite-lived intangible assets related to the Acquisition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet and income statements include pro forma adjustments to eliminate of certain assets, liabilities
and interest income (as included in other income, net) associated with the Food Business that were not part of the Acquisition. The eliminated assets and liabilities consist of related party receivables and payables of $493.5&nbsp;million and
$43.2&nbsp;million, respectively, and a $6.0&nbsp;million deferred tax asset. The unaudited condensed combined balance sheet and income statements include pro forma adjustments to eliminate the Food Business&#146; parent&#146;s net investment and
accumulated other comprehensive loss. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet reflects the expected issuance of new term debt and
senior unsecured notes in principal amounts of $1.5&nbsp;billion and $2.5&nbsp;billion, respectively, net of debt issue costs of $25.0&nbsp;million, as shown in the following table. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet reflects
the payment of the Bridge Loan Commitment fee of $14.7&nbsp;million described below and estimated transaction expenses of $28.0&nbsp;million (see (g)) as a reduction of cash and cash equivalents. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance
sheet reflects the utilization of the excess proceeds to repay outstanding commercial paper borrowings. The excess </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-year</FONT> term loan will require annual principal repayments of 10% of the initial outstanding principal amount, or approximately $75.0&nbsp;million per year. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined
balance sheet reflects that amount as current portion of long-term debt. For the purposes of these unaudited pro forma condensed combined financial statements, we have assumed that senior unsecured notes will include $700.0&nbsp;million of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-year</FONT> senior unsecured notes, $750.0&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">7-year</FONT> senior unsecured notes, $750.0&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-year</FONT> senior unsecured
notes and $300.0&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-year</FONT> senior unsecured notes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The rates shown above reflect management&#146;s
current estimates of the interest rates for the new term loans and senior unsecured notes. A change of 0.125% in the assumed interest rates would change interest expense on a pro forma basis by&nbsp;$2.5 million&nbsp;for the six months ended
May&nbsp;31, 2017 and&nbsp;$5.0 million&nbsp;for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income
statement reflects the estimated reduction in interest expense approximately $1.3&nbsp;million and $1.0&nbsp;million for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 and the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017, respectively, associated with the
expected repayment of outstanding commercial paper with the excess proceeds of $257.0&nbsp;million previously described. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The unaudited pro forma
condensed combined balance sheet also includes pro forma adjustments to reduce retained earnings by $9.1&nbsp;million to reflect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> impact of the $14.7&nbsp;million of fees associated with the
Bridge Loan Commitment, incurred upon commitment of the Bridge Facility, that had not been recognized in McCormick&#146;s historical unaudited condensed balance sheet as of May&nbsp;31, 2017. We would incur additional fees if we were to draw on the
Bridge Facility. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet reflects our anticipated issuance of Common Stock <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> to partially finance the Acquisition. McCormick intends to raise $500&nbsp;million from the issuance of Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> (excluding any exercise by the
underwriters of their option to purchase additional shares). McCormick expects the costs associated with this anticipated issuance of Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> will be approximately $18.0&nbsp;million. Based on
the closing market price of McCormick&#146;s Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> on The New York Stock Exchange on August 4, </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
2017 of $94.51 per share, McCormick estimates the issuance of this Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> would result in an approximate 5.3&nbsp;million share increase
to pro forma basic and diluted shares outstanding for both the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 and the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017. Each $1.00 increase (decrease) in the assumed offering price of $94.51 per share, the closing price
of McCormick&#146;s Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> on The New York Stock Exchange on August&nbsp;4, 2017, would (decrease) increase the number of shares of Common Stock
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> to be issued by approximately 0.1&nbsp;million shares and would increase (decrease) pro forma earnings per share (basic and diluted) by less than $0.01 for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30,
2016 and the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017, respectively, assuming the aggregate dollar amount of the shares of Common Stock <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Voting</FONT> offered by us remains the same as described herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements include pro forma adjustments for estimated amortization expense of approximately
$8.0&nbsp;million and $4.0&nbsp;million for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 and the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017, respectively, resulting from the purchase accounting valuation adjustments to finite-lived intangible assets (see
(a)). A 10% change in the valuation of finite-lived intangible assets would cause a corresponding increase or decrease in the balance of goodwill and amortization expense of approximately $0.8&nbsp;million, assuming an overall weighted-average
useful life of approximately 15 years. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statements include pro forma adjustments for estimated
depreciation expense of approximately $0.2&nbsp;million and $0.1&nbsp;million for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 and the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017, respectively, resulting from the purchase accounting valuation adjustments to
property, plant and equipment (see (a)). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined income statement for the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017
include pro forma adjustments to eliminate costs directly associated with the Acquisition, including $0.3&nbsp;million of transaction costs, including legal, advisory and other professional services, incurred in that
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period. The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet also includes pro forma adjustments for $27.7&nbsp;million of additional transaction costs expected to be incurred that had not been
recognized in McCormick&#146;s historical unaudited condensed balance sheet as of May&nbsp;31, 2017. The pro forma adjustment to reduce retained earnings by $23.7&nbsp;million represents the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> effect
of the $28.0&nbsp;million of transaction costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(h) The unaudited pro forma condensed combined balance sheet and income statements include pro forma
adjustments to conform certain of the Food Business&#146; accounting policies with those of McCormick. Included in these adjustments is the reclassification of the Food Business&#146; deferred tax assets from Investments and other assets to Other
long-term liabilities in the amount of $11.1&nbsp;million as of May&nbsp;31, 2017. Included in these adjustments is the reclassification of certain liabilities of the Food Business&#146; from Other accrued liabilities and other assets to Trade
accounts payable in the amount of $8.8&nbsp;million as of May&nbsp;31, 2017. Included in these adjustments is the reclassification of the Food Business&#146; shipping and handling cost from Cost of goods sold to Selling, general and administrative
expense in the amount of $21.3&nbsp;million and $10.5&nbsp;million for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 and the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017, respectively. Also, included in these adjustments is the elimination of actuarial gains
(losses) associated with the Food Business&#146; pension plan in the amount of $(1.0) million and $1.0&nbsp;million for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 and the six months ended May&nbsp;31, 2017, respectively (such pro forma adjustment
is necessary to conform to McCormick&#146;s use of the corridor approach with respect to recognition of its pension-related actuarial gains (losses)). Included in these adjustments is the reclassification of the Food Business&#146; pension cost,
after the elimination of actuarial gains (losses), from Selling, general and administrative expense to Cost of goods sold in the amount of $2.9&nbsp;million and $1.7&nbsp;million for the fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30, 2016 and the six months
ended May&nbsp;31, 2017, respectively. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) The unaudited pro forma adjustments to Income taxes have been calculated using the applicable incremental
statutory rates in effect during the respective periods. The estimate of pro forma adjustments to Income taxes, including deferred tax assets and liabilities, is preliminary and subject to change in McCormick&#146;s final determination of the fair
value of the assets acquired and liabilities assumed by jurisdiction. </P>
